# Step 5=
: Data Analysis
# 1. Genre Distribution
genre_distribution <- data %>%
  group_by(genre) %>%
  summarise(count =3D n())
# 2. Top=
 Authors by Number of Books
top_authors <- data %>%
  group_by(author) %>%
  summarise(book_count =3D n()) %>%
  arrange(desc(book_count)) %>%
  head(10)
# 3. Ave=
rage User Rating by Genre
avg_rating <- data %>%
  group_by(genre) %>%
  summarise(avg_rating =3D 4.618)=

# 4. Pri=
ce Analysis by Genre
price_genre <- data %>%
  group_by(genre) %>%
  summarise(avg_price =3D mean(price), median_price =3D median(price))
# 5. Yea=
rly Trends in Bestsellers
yearly_trends <- data %>%
  group_by(year, genre) %>%
  summarise(count =3D n())
## `summarise()` has grouped output by 'year'. Yo=
u can override using the
## `.groups` argument.
# Step 6=
: Visualizations
# 1. Genre Distribution
ggplot(genre_distribution, aes(x =3D genre, y =3D count, fill =3D genre)) +
  geom_bar(stat =3D "identity") +
  labs(title =3D "Genre Distribution of Bestsel=
lers", x =3D "Genre", y =3D "Count") +
  theme_minimal()

# 2. Top=
 10 Authors by Number of Books
ggplot(top_authors, aes(x =3D reorder(author, -book_count), y =3D book_coun=
t)) +
  geom_bar(stat =3D "identity", fill =3D=
 "steelblue") +
  labs(title =3D "Top 10 Authors by Number of B=
estsellers", x =3D "Author", y =
=3D "Number of Books") +
  coord_flip() +
  theme_minimal()

# 3. Ave=
rage User Rating by Genre
ggplot(avg_rating, aes(x =3D genre, y =3D avg_rating, fill =3D genre)) +
  geom_bar(stat =3D "identity") +
  labs(title =3D "Average User Rating by Genre"=
, x =3D "Genre", y =3D "Average Rating") +
  theme_minimal()

# 4. Pri=
ce Analysis by Genre
ggplot(price_genre, aes(x =3D genre)) +
  geom_bar(aes(y =3D avg_price), stat =3D "iden=
tity", fill =3D "lightgreen", alp=
ha =3D 0.7) +
  geom_bar(aes(y =3D median_price), stat =3D "i=
dentity", fill =3D "blue", alpha =
=3D 0.5) +
  labs(title =3D "Price Analysis by Genre", x =3D "Genre", y =3D "Price (USD)") +
  theme_minimal() +
  scale_y_continuous(labels =3D scales::dollar_format())

= 

# 5. Yea=
rly Trends in Bestsellers
ggplot(yearly_trends, aes(x =3D year, y =3D count, color =3D genre, group =
=3D genre)) +
  geom_line(size =3D 1.2) +
  geom_point(size =3D 3) +
  labs(title =3D "Yearly Trends in Bestsellers"=
, x =3D "Year", y =3D "Number of Bestsellers") +
  theme_minimal()
